    CAL  : Target of routine calibration plan

    B    : Target accepted for AO-1/AO-2 with priority B
    GT   : Target of guaranteed time program
    T(*) : Triggered target candidate accepted for AO-1/2 with priority A or B

Most of the up-dates reflect corrected positions (< 1 arcmin).
